Sisense?</h2><div class="industry-cards-styles__CardsContainer-sc-84e55258-2 bIJHw"><div class="industry-cards-styles__CardsRow-sc-84e55258-3 hxjvaP"><div class="card-styles__Container-sc-b7cd277b-0 class="card-styles__Text-sc-b7cd277b-6 dPHdZs">Sisense is the pioneer of infused analytics — a new way for companies to unleash the power of data to transform the way they work, enhance the customer experience, and grow their business. Every day our 2,000+ customers use the Sisense platform to empower people, transform their businesses, disrupt markets, and even change peoples’ lives.</p></div></div><div class="card-styles__Container-sc-b7cd277b-0 jfYSou"><div class="card-styles__WrapperContainer-sc-b7cd277b-1 dNBtxk"><div class="card-styles__TopContainer-sc-b7cd277b-2 dqvMIk"><div class="card-styles__IconContainer-sc-b7cd277b-3 jHIetT"><img src="https://cdn.sisense.com/wp-content/uploads/community-1-1.svg" class="card-styles__Icon-sc-b7cd277b-4 gPZaFH"/></div><p class="card-styles__Title-sc-b7cd277b-5 fusSVP">People first</p></div><p class="card-styles__Text-sc-b7cd277b-6 dPHdZs">Sisense is more than just a technology business. We’re a people business. Our team is our most valuable resource, and it’s why we prioritize our people over everything and why we promote employee wellbeing. Every quarter we ask all of our employees to take a break and “come up for air” and we also give company-wide self-care days to help disconnect from the added stresses of the new reality of remote working.</p></div></div><div class="card-styles__Container-sc-b7cd277b-0 jfYSou"><div class="card-styles__WrapperContainer-sc-b7cd277b-1 dNBtxk"><div class="card-styles__TopContainer-sc-b7cd277b-2 dqvMIk"><div class="card-styles__IconContainer-sc-b7cd277b-3 jHIetT"><img src="https://cdn.sisense.com/wp-content/uploads/customer-obsessed-2.svg" class="card-styles__Icon-sc-b7cd277b-4 gPZaFH"/></div><p class="card-styles__Title-sc-b7cd277b-5 fusSVP">Career accelerator</p></div><p class="card-styles__Text-sc-b7cd277b-6 dPHdZs">Accelerate your career through the Sisense journey, and accomplish more than you ever believed possible. Our managers focus on the growth of each employee at every point in our Talk Growth feedback and assessment program.
